function RgetCity(city_code){
$.get(siteurl+"esen-api/ramazan/"+city_code,function(a){var t=new Date,r=jQuery.parseJSON(a),e=r.bugun.aksam,i=r.yarin.imsak,h=e.split(":"),s=i.split(":");tarih_iftar=RtarihYap(h[0],h[1]),tarih_sahur=RtarihYap(s[0],s[1]),tarih_sahur1=RtarihYap(s[0],s[1]),tarih_sahur.setDate(tarih_sahur.getDate()),tarih_sahur1.setDate(tarih_sahur.getDate()+1);setInterval(function(){var a=(new Date).getTime();if(tarih_iftar>t&&t>tarih_sahur){var r=tarih_iftar;$(".ramazan-detay-text").text("İÇİN İFTAR VAKTİNE KALAN SÜRE")}else if(tarih_sahur1>tarih_iftar&&tarih_sahur1>t){$(".ramazan-detay-text").text("İÇİN SAHUR VAKTİNE KALAN SÜRE");r=tarih_sahur1}else if(tarih_sahur<tarih_iftar&&tarih_sahur>t){$(".ramazan-detay-text").text("İÇİN SAHUR VAKTİNE KALAN SÜRE");r=tarih_sahur}else $(".ramazan-detay-text").text("HAYIRLI RAMAZANLAR"),r=null;var e=r-a,i=(Math.floor(e/864e5),Math.floor(e%864e5/36e5)),h=Math.floor(e%36e5/6e4),s=Math.floor(e%6e4/1e3);i=i<10?"0"+i:i,h=h<10?"0"+h:h,s=s<10?"0"+s:s,$(".ramazan-countdown").text(i+":"+h+":"+s),e<0&&$(".ramazan-countdown").text("BURSA İÇİN İFTAR VAKTİ")},1e3)});
}

});

<script type="167a3b515225315b77392708-text/javascript">var nextSlotId=0;
function generateNextSlotName(){
var id=nextSlotId++;
return 'manset_ads' + id;
}
function addNewSlot(name, size){
var slotName=generateNextSlotName();
googletag.cmd.push(function(){
var slot=googletag.defineSlot(name, size, slotName).
setTargeting("AnaMansetAdvortial","infinitescroll").
addService(googletag.pubads());
googletag.display("manset_ads");
googletag.pubads().refresh([slot]);
});
return false;
}</script>

<script type="167a3b515225315b77392708-text/javascript">$(document).ready(function(){
$('#quick-details > .close').on('click', function(){
$('#quick-details').removeClass('active');
$('#quick-details > .content').html('');
})
$('.quick-onizle').on('click', function(){
var this_postid=$(this).attr('data-postid');
$.ajax({
url:siteurl+"esen-api/author-post/detail",
data:{
post_id: this_postid
},
type:'get',
beforeSend:function(xhr){
},
success:function(data){
if(data){
$('#quick-details > .content').append(data);
$('#quick-details').addClass('active');
}else{
}}
});
})
});</script>

<script type="167a3b515225315b77392708-text/javascript">$(function(){
$('.puan-durumu-current').on('click', function(){
$(".euro-puan-durumu").toggleClass('active');
if($(".puan-durumu-current > i.fa").hasClass('fa-chevron-down')){
$(".puan-durumu-current > i.fa").addClass('fa-chevron-up');
$(".puan-durumu-current > i.fa").removeClass('fa-chevron-down');
}else{
$(".puan-durumu-current > i.fa").removeClass('fa-chevron-up');
$(".puan-durumu-current > i.fa").addClass('fa-chevron-down');
}});
$('.euro-puan-durumu > li').on('click', function(){
var index=$(this).index();
var selected=$(this).data('value');
var type=$(this).data('type');
$.ajax({
type: 'GET',
url: esenhaber.ajax_url,
data: {
'action': 'ajax_puan',
'select':  'puan',
'lig': type,
'full': '',
},
success: function(data){
$('.puan-icerik').html(data);
}});
//$('.euro-puan-durumu > li').removeClass('active');
//$(this).addClass('active');
//$('.puan-icerik').removeClass('active');
$('.puan-icerik:eq('+index+')').addClass('active');
$(".euro-puan-durumu").toggleClass('active');
$('.puan-durumu-current').html(selected + ' <i class="fa fa-chevron-down"></i>');
});
});</script>

<script type="167a3b515225315b77392708-text/javascript">var fixOwl=function(){
var $stage=$('.owl-stage'),
stageW=$stage.width(),
$el=$('.owl-item'),
elW=0;
$el.each(function(){
elW +=$(this).width()+ +($(this).css("margin-right").slice(0, -2))
});
if(elW > stageW){
$stage.width(elW);
};}
$(function(){
var owl=$('.owl-699d90c5a11b2').owlCarousel({
loop:false,
margin:25,
onInitialized: fixOwl,
onRefreshed: fixOwl,
nav:false,
dots:false,
slideBy:3,
autoplay:false,
autoplaySpeed:500,
autoplayTimeout:4500,
items:1,
singleItem: true,
autoplayHoverPause:true,
navSpeed:500,
responsive:{
0:{
items:2,
dots:true,
},
768:{
items:3,
dots:true,
},
1000:{

}}
});

});
$('.slider-nav-699d90c5a11b2 .slide-right').on('click', function(){
owl.trigger('next.owl.carousel',500);
});
$('.slider-nav-699d90c5a11b2 .slide-left').mouseover(function(){
owl.trigger('stop.owl.autoplay');
});

owl.trigger('play.owl.autoplay');
});

var fixOwl=function(){
var $stage=$('.owl-stage'),
stageW=$stage.width(),
$el=$('.owl-item'),
elW=0;
$el.each(function(){
elW +=$(this).width()+ +($(this).css("margin-right").slice(0, -2))
});
if(elW > stageW){
$stage.width(elW);
};}
$(function(){
var fikstur_owl=$('.owl-ozel-fiksturler').owlCarousel({
loop:true,
margin:25,
onInitialized: fixOwl,
onRefreshed: fixOwl,
nav:false,
dots:false,
slideBy:1,
autoplay:false,
autoplaySpeed:500,
autoplayTimeout:4500,
items:2,
singleItem: true,
navSpeed:500,
responsive:{
0:{
items:2,
dots:true,
slideBy:2,
},
768:{

slideBy:1,
},

items:5,

slideBy:1,
}}
});

});
$('.slider-nav-ozel-fiksturler .slide-right').on('click', function(){

});

current_week_index=0 ;

}
fikstur_owl.trigger('to.owl.carousel', current_week_index);

return false;

},

});
